        <div class="item-description">
                <h2>Description</h2>
                <div class="item-excerpt trunc" itemprop="description" data-height="230">

                    The first book in The Inheritance Series <br />
                    <br />
                    When poor farm boy Eragon finds a polished stone in the forest, he thinks it&#039;s a lucky discovery. Perhaps, he will be able to buy his family food for the winter. <br />
                    <br />
                    But, when a baby dragon hatches out of the stone, Eragon realises he&#039;s stumbled upon a legacy nearly as old as the Empire itself. <br />
                    <br />
                    His simple life is shattered, and he&#039;s thrust into a perilous new world of destiny, magic and power. To navigate this dark terrain, and survive his cruel king&#039;s evil ways, he must take up the mantle of the legendary Dragon Riders. <br />
                    <br />
                    Will he succeed? The fate of the Empire rests in his hands. . .<br />
                    <a class='read-more'>show more</a>
                </div>
            </div>

                        <h2>About Christopher Paolini</h2>
                        <div class="block text-block trunc" data-height="100">
                            Christopher Paolini was educated at home by his parents. His abiding love of fantasy and science fiction inspired him to begin writing his debut novel, Eragon, when he graduated from high school at fifteen. He became a New York Times bestselling author at nineteen. Christopher lives in Montana, USA, where the dramatic landscape fed his vision of Alagaesia. Inheritance, the final book in the sequence, was published in November 2011.<br />
